<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>17th century organ music from a manuscript (N°888, cote 153D), preserved at the Library of the University in Liège, Belgium.<br />
In English: 'Book of the Cross-bearing Brothers of Liège'.
</p><p>Includes 54 works by:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Category:Gabrieli,_Andrea" title="Category:Gabrieli, Andrea">Andrea Gabrieli</a>
</li><li>Petro Philippi (<a href="/wiki/Category:Philips,_Peter" title="Category:Philips, Peter">Peter Philips</a>)
</li><li>Jean Piere Swelinck (<a href="/wiki/Category:Sweelinck,_Jan_Pieterszoon" title="Category:Sweelinck, Jan Pieterszoon">Jan Pieterszoon Sweelinck</a>)
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Category:Merulo,_Claudio" title="Category:Merulo, Claudio">Claudio Merulo</a>
</li><li>Wilhelmo Brouno (<a href="/wiki/Category:Browne,_William" title="Category:Browne, William">William Browne</a>)
</li><li>Frater Gerardus Scronx (<a href="/wiki/Category:Scronx,_Gerardus" title="Category:Scronx, Gerardus">Gerardus Scronx</a>)
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Category:Striggio,_Alessandro" title="Category:Striggio, Alessandro">Alessandro Striggio</a>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Category:Pellegrini,_Vincenzo" title="Category:Pellegrini, Vincenzo">Vincenzo Pellegrini</a>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Category:Erbach,_Christian" title="Category:Erbach, Christian">Christian Erbach</a>
</li><li><a href="/wiki/Category:Siefert,_Paul" title="Category:Siefert, Paul">Paul Siefert</a>
</li><li>and by unknown composer(s)
</li></ul>
